♠❛t❤❡♠❛t✐❝❛❧ ♠❡t❤♦❞s ❛♥❞ ❛❧❣♦r✐t❤♠s❄  ■t ✐s ❛❧s♦ r❡❧❛t❡❞ t♦ t❤❡ ❝♦♠♣❧❡①✐t② ♦❢

♦♥ t❤❡ ✐♥t❡r❢❛❝❡ ✉s❡❞ ❜② ❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs✳  ❆s ❛ r❡s✉❧t✱ ✐t t❛❦❡s t❤r❡❡ t♦ ✜✈❡ ♠✐♥✉t❡s
❢♦r ❡❛❝❤ ✉s❡r t♦ ❣❡♥❡r❛t❡ ♦♥❡ ❞❛t❛ ♣♦✐♥t✳

♣♦r❛t❡ ❛♥❞ ♠❛❝r♦❡❝♦♥♦♠✐❝ ❡✈❡♥ts✱ ✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦rs ♦❢ ❝❡rt❛✐♥ ♣r✐❝❡ ❧❡✈❡❧s ❜❡✐♥❣
r❡❛❝❤❡❞✱ ❛♥❞ ✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦rs ♦❢ t❤❡ ♣r♦❜❛❜✐❧✐t② ♦❢ s✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥t ❡✈❡♥ts ✐♥✢✉❡♥❝✐♥❣

■♥t❡❧❧✐❣❡♥❝❡  ✐♥ tr❛❞✐t✐♦♥❛❧  ♠❛r❦❡ts✳                                                       ■t  ❝❛♥  ❛❧s♦  ❜❡ tr❡❛t❡❞  ❛s  ♣r♦t❡❝t✐✈❡

t❤❡ ❝r②♣t♦♠❛r❦❡t✱ ❛ ♣♦rt✐♦♥ ♦❢ t❤❡ ❢✉♥❞s ♠❛② ❜❡ tr❛♥s❢❡rr❡❞ t♦ ❝r②♣t♦❛s✲
s❡ts ✇✐t❤ t❤❡ ♣✉r♣♦s❡ ♦❢ ❡❛r♥✐♥❣ ❛ ♣r♦✜t ✉♣♦♥ t❤❡ r❡❤❛❜✐❧✐t❛t✐♦♥ ♦❢ t❤❛t
♠❛r❦❡t✳  ❙❉ ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡ ✉s❡❞ ❛s ❛ ❜❡♥❝❤♠❛r❦ t♦ ❡st✐♠❛t❡ t❤❡ r❡s✉❧ts✳
❆❝t✐✈❡ ♠❛♥❛❣❡♠❡♥t ♦❢ t❤❡ t❤✐r❞ ♣❛rt ♦❢ t❤❡ ♣♦rt❢♦❧✐♦ ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡❣✐♥ ✇✐t❤✐♥ ❛ ❢❡✇
♠♦♥t❤s ❛❢t❡r t❤❡ ❡♥❞ ♦❢ t❤❡ ❚♦❦❡♥ ❙❛❧❡✳  ❚♦ ❞♦ t❤✐s✱  ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ♥❡❡❞ t♦ ❝♦♠♣❧❡t❡
t❤❡ ♣r❡♣❛r❛t✐♦♥ ♦❢ t❤❡ ❡♥t✐r❡ tr❛❞✐♥❣ ✐♥❢r❛str✉❝t✉r❡✱ s✉❝❤ ❛s ❛❝❝♦✉♥ts ❛♥❞ ❧❡❣❛❧
str✉❝t✉r❡  ✭✐t  ✐s  ♥❡❝❡ss❛r② t♦  ❡st❛❜❧✐s❤  ❛ s❡♣❛r❛t❡  ❧❡❣❛❧  ❡♥t✐t②  ❢♦r t❤❡  ❢✉♥❞  ❛♥❞
t♦ ♦❜t❛✐♥ t❤❡ ♥❡❝❡ss❛r② ❧✐❝❡♥s❡s✮✳
❚❤✐s ♣♦rt❢♦❧✐♦ ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡ ♠❛♥❛❣❡❞ ❜② ♦✉r t❡❛♠ ♦❢ tr❛❞❡rs ❛♥❞ tr❛❞✐♥❣ r♦❜♦ts✱
✇❤♦ ✇✐❧❧ ✉s❡ t❤❡ ❞❛t❛✱ s✐❣♥❛❧s✱ ❛♥❞ ❛♥❛❧②t✐❝s ♦❜t❛✐♥❡❞ t❤r♦✉❣❤ t❤❡ ❍②❜r✐❞ ■♥✲
t❡❧❧✐❣❡♥❝❡ t❡❝❤♥♦❧♦❣②✳  ❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❛♣♣❧② ✈❛r✐♦✉s str❛t❡❣✐❡s ✐♥ t❤❡ ✜♥❛♥❝✐❛❧ ♠❛r❦❡ts
✭❜♦t❤  ❝r②♣t♦  ❛♥❞ tr❛❞✐t✐♦♥❛❧✮  ✇✐t❤✐♥  ❞✐✛❡r❡♥t t✐♠❡  ❤♦r✐③♦♥s✱  ❢r♦♠ s❤♦rt✲t❡r♠
tr❛❞❡s t♦  ❧♦♥❣✲t❡r♠  ✐♥✈❡st♠❡♥ts✳                                                           ❚❤❡  ❝❤♦✐❝❡  ♦❢ str❛t❡❣②  ❛♥❞  ❛ss❡ts  ✐♥✈❡st❡❞
✇✐❧❧ ❞r❛✇ ♦♥ ❛ ♣♦s✐t✐✈❡ ❡✈❛❧✉❛t✐♦♥ ❢r♦♠ ❍②❜r✐❞ ■♥t❡❧❧✐❣❡♥❝❡✱ ❛s ✇❡❧❧ ❛s s✉❝❝❡ss✲
❢✉❧ t❡st✐♥❣ ✐♥ t❤❡ ❢♦r♠ ♦❢ ❜❛❝❦ ❛♥❞ ❢♦r✇❛r❞ t❡sts✳
✶✶




❖✉r t❡❛♠ ✇✐❧❧ ♣r❡♣❛r❡ ❞❡t❛✐❧❡❞ ♠♦♥t❤❧② r❡♣♦rts ❢❡❛t✉r✐♥❣ t❤❡ r❡s✉❧ts ♦❢ t❤❡
tr❛❞❡s ❡①❡❝✉t❡❞ ❛♥❞ ♠❛❦❡ t❤❡♠ ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ t♦ t❤❡ ❝♦♠♠✉♥✐t②✳
✹✳✹                                                                                        ❈◆❉ ♣♦♦❧  ❢♦r  ❞②♥❛♠✐❝  ❝♦♠♣❡♥s❛t✐♦♥  ♦❢  ❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs
❚♦ ❢♦r♠ ❛ st❡❛❞✐❧② ❣r♦✇✐♥❣ ✐♥t❡r♥❛❧ ❡❝♦♥♦♠②✱ ❈✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦r ✇✐❧❧ ❝r❡❛t❡ t❤❡ ✐♥t❡r♥❛❧
♠♦t✐✈❛t✐♦♥❛❧ ♣♦♦❧ ♦❢ ❈◆❉ t♦❦❡♥s✳
❚❤❡ ♣♦♦❧ t♦❦❡♥s ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡ ✉s❡❞ t♦ ❡♥❝♦✉r❛❣❡ t❤❡ ❈✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦r ❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs✱ ❛s ✇❡❧❧
❛s ♦t❤❡r ❝♦♥tr✐❜✉t♦rs t♦ t❤❡ ❡❝♦s②st❡♠✱ ✇❤♦ ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡ ❜r✐♥❣✐♥❣ s✐❣♥✐✜❝❛♥t ✈❛❧✉❡s t♦
t❤❡ ❡❝♦s②st❡♠ ♦❢ ❍②❜r✐❞ ■♥t❡❧❧✐❣❡♥❝❡ ✭s❝✐❡♥t✐sts✱ ✈✐s✐♦♥❛r✐❡s✱ ❡♥❣✐♥❡❡rs✱ tr❛❞❡rs✱
✐♥✈❡st♦rs✱ ♠❛r❦❡t❡rs✱ ✈❡♥❞♦rs✱ ❡t❝✳✮✳
❋♦r t❤❡  ❝♦♥tr✐❜✉t♦rs t♦  ❜❡  ❡♥❝♦✉r❛❣❡❞✱  ❈◆❉  ♣♦♦❧ t♦❦❡♥s  ✇✐❧❧  ❜❡  ❜r♦✉❣❤t
t♦ t❤❡ ♣♦♦❧ ♣r✐♠❛r✐❧② ❢r♦♠ s❡❧❧✐♥❣ ♦❢ t❤❡ ❈✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦r ❛♥❛❧②t✐❝❛❧ ♣r♦❞✉❝ts ✲ t❤♦s❡
♣r♦❞✉❝ts ❛♥❞ t❡❝❤♥♦❧♦❣✐❡s t❤❛t ✇✐❧❧ ❜❡ ❛✈❛✐❧❛❜❧❡ ♦♥❧② t❤r♦✉❣❤ t❤❡ s❛❧❡ ♦❢ ❈◆❉
t♦❦❡♥s ❜② ❈✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦r ❝♦♠♣❛♥②✳
✹✳✺                                                                                        ❊❚❍✴❇❚❈  ♣♦♦❧  ❢♦r  ❞②♥❛♠✐❝  ❝♦♠♣❡♥s❛t✐♦♥
♦❢  ❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs
❊✈❡r② q✉❛rt❡r ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ r❡❝♦r❞ t❤❡ r❡s✉❧ts ♦❢ ❛❧❧ t❤❡ ❛❝❝♦✉♥ts ✐♥ t❤❡ ❍②❜r✐❞ ■♥t❡❧❧✐✲
❣❡♥❝❡ ♣♦rt❢♦❧✐♦ ✐♥ ♦r❞❡r t♦ ❢♦r♠ ❛ ❞②♥❛♠✐❝ ♠♦t✐✈❛t✐♦♥❛❧ ❊❚❍✴❇❚❈ ♣♦♦❧✱ ❞❡s✐❣✲
♥❛t❡❞ t♦ r❡✇❛r❞ ❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs ❢♦r t❤❡✐r ✐♥t❡❧❧❡❝t✉❛❧ ✐♥✈❡st♠❡♥t ✐♥t♦ t❤❡ ❡❝♦s②st❡♠✳
■♥ t❤❡ ❝❛s❡ ♦❢ ♣♦s✐t✐✈❡ ♣❡r❢♦r♠❛♥❝❡ ✭r❡❧❛t✐✈❡ t♦ t❤❡ ✐♥✐t✐❛❧ st❛t❡ ♦❢ t❤❡ ♣♦rt✲
❢♦❧✐♦✮✱ ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❞✐str✐❜✉t❡ t❤❡ ♣r♦✜t ❛s ❢♦❧❧♦✇s✿
✶✳                                                                                         ✪ ✇✐❧❧ r❡♠❛✐♥ ✐♥ t❤❡ ❍②❜r✐❞ ■♥t❡❧❧✐❣❡♥❝❡ ♣♦rt❢♦❧✐♦✱ ❡♥s✉r✐♥❣ ✐ts ❣r♦✇t❤
❢♦r t❤❡ ♥❡①t r❡♣♦rt✐♥❣ ♣❡r✐♦❞❀
✷✳                                                                                         ✪ ✐s t❤❡ ♣❡r❢♦r♠❛♥❝❡ ❢❡❡ ❢♦r t❤❡ ❈✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦r t❡❛♠ ✭t♦ ❜❡ ♣❛✐❞ ♦♥❧② ✐❢ t❤❡
♣♦rt❢♦❧✐♦ s✐③❡ ✐s ❧❛r❣❡r t❤❛♥ ✐ts ✐♥✐t✐❛❧ st❛t❡✮❀
✸✳                                                                                         ✪ ✲ ❢✉♥❞s t♦ r❡♣❧❡♥✐s❤ t❤❡ ❞②♥❛♠✐❝ ♠♦t✐✈❛t✐♦♥❛❧ ❊❚❍✴❇❚❈ ♣♦♦❧✳
■♥ ❝❛s❡ ♦❢ ❛ ❧♦ss✱ ✇❡ ✇✐❧❧ ❝❛♥ ✉s❡ t❤❡ r❡s❡r✈❡ ❢✉♥❞ t♦ ♣r♦✈✐❞❡ ✜♥❛♥❝✐❛❧ ♠♦t✐✲
✈❛t✐♦♥ ❛♥❞ ❝♦♠♣❡♥s❛t✐♦♥ t♦ t❤❡ s✉♣❡r❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs ❢♦r t❤❡ ♣❡r✐♦❞ ✐♥ q✉❡st✐♦♥✳
❚❤❡  ♣❛rt✐❡s  ❛❝❦♥♦✇❧❡❞❣❡ t❤❛t t❤❡  ❝✉rr❡♥t st❛t❡  ♦❢ t❤❡  ❝r②♣t♦❝✉rr❡♥❝②  ✐♥✲
❞✉str② ✐s ✉♥❝❡rt❛✐♥ ❞✉❡ t♦ ❢❛st ❝❤❛♥❣✐♥❣ r❡❣✉❧❛t✐♦♥s ❛♥❞✴♦r ❧❛❝❦ ♦❢ r❡❣✉❧❛t♦r②
❝❡rt❛✐♥t②  ✐♥ s❡✈❡r❛❧  ❥✉r✐s❞✐❝t✐♦♥s✳                                                      ❚♦  ❝♦♠♣❧②  ✇✐t❤  ❛♥② r❡❣✉❧❛t✐♦♥s  ❛♥❞✴♦r t♦
❡♥s✉r❡  ✈✐❛❜✐❧✐t②  ♦❢  ✐ts  ❜✉s✐♥❡ss  ♠♦❞❡❧  ✐♥  ❧✐❣❤t  ♦❢  ❛♥②  ♠❛r❦❡t✱  t❡❝❤♥♦❧♦❣✐❝❛❧✱
❛♥❞✴♦r r❡❣✉❧❛t♦r② ❝❤❛♥❣❡s✱ ❈♦♠♣❛♥② r❡s❡r✈❡s t❤❡ r✐❣❤t t♦ ❛♠❡♥❞✱ s✉♣♣❧❡♠❡♥t✱
♦r  ❞❡❧❡t❡  ❛♥② t❡r♠  ♦❢ t❤✐s  ❆❣r❡❡♠❡♥t✱  ✐♥❝❧✉❞✐♥❣  ❜✉t  ♥♦t  ❧✐♠✐t❡❞ t♦  ❛♥② t❡r♠s
❞❡❛❧✐♥❣ ✇✐t❤ t❤❡ ❝r❡❛t✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❞②♥❛♠✐❝ ♠♦t✐✈❛t✐♦♥❛❧ ♣♦♦❧s✳
✹✳✻                                                                                        ▼♦♥❡t✐s❛t✐♦♥  ♦❢  ✐♥t❡❧❧❡❝t✉❛❧  ❝♦♥tr✐❜✉t✐♦♥  ♦❢
❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs
❋♦r❡❝❛st❡rs  ❢♦r♠✐♥❣ t❤❡  ❈✐♥❞✐❝❛t♦r  ❝♦❧❧❡❝t✐✈❡  ✐♥t❡❧❧✐❣❡♥❝❡  ❛r❡ t❤❡  ❦❡②  ❡❧❡♠❡♥t
t♦  ❜❡  ❝r❡❛t❡❞  ✇✐t❤  ✐♥ t❤❡  ❡❝♦s②st❡♠✳                                                  ❚❤❡ s✉❝❝❡ss❢✉❧  ♦♣❡r❛t✐♦♥  ♦❢ t❤✐s s②st❡♠
❛s ❛ ✇❤♦❧❡ r❡q✉✐r❡s t❤❡ ♣❡rs♦♥❛❧ ♠♦t✐✈❛t✐♦♥ ♦❢ ❢♦r❡❝❛st❡rs t♦ ❜❡ s✉st❛✐♥❡❞✱ ❛♥❞

❖✉r ♠♦❞❡❧s ❛r❡ ♦♣t✐♠✐s❡❞ ❛♥❞ ❜❛❝❦ t❡st✲❛ss✐st❡❞ ❞✉❡ t♦ t❤❡ ♣✐♣❡❧✐♥❡s ✐♥✈♦❧✈❡❞✳
